The game and its variants are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nParchisi originated in India by the 6th century. \r\n\r\nEach player rolls the die; the highest roller begins the game. Players alternate turns in a clockwise direction.\r\n\r\nLudo can be played by two, three, or four, without partnerships. To enter a token into play from its yard to its starting square, a player must roll a 6. If the player has no tokens yet in play and rolls other than a 6, the turn passes to the next player. Once a player has one or more tokens in play, he selects a token and moves it forwards along the track the number of squares indicated by the dice. Players must always move a token according to the die value rolled. Passes are not allowed; if no move is possible, the turn moves to the next player.\r\n\r\nPlayers may not end their move on a square they already occupy. When matched, clears the entire column it is on.\r\n✓\tBy matching 4 jewels of the same color in one column and 3 jewels in one row or vice versa you get a cross buster. When matched, clears the entire row and column it is on.\r\n✓\tIf you are able to match 5 jewels, you get a super jewel. This can be switched with any other single jewel on the board. When activated, all the same-colored jewels as the jewel it was switched with, will be removed from the board. If you combine the jewel with a special jewel, all the jewels of that color will change into that special jewel, and activate those special jewels.\r\n✓\tBy matching 5 jewels of the same color in one column and 3 jewels in one row or vice versa you get a super cross jewel. This can be switched with any other single jewel on the board. When activated, all the same-colored jewels will transform into cross busters and activate those jewels.\r\n✓\tWhen you destroy a line of three you receive 10 points for each jewel in the line. If you destroy two separate lines of three you receive 20 points for each jewel in the line. When you destroy a line of 4 you receive 100 points for each jewel in the line.\r\n✓\tWhen you switch on a row buster or column buster the base score for each jewel is 60 points.\r\n✓\tWhen you explode a super jewel the base score for each jewel is 100 points.\r\n✓\tWhen you explode a jewel bomb the base score is 40 points.\r\n✓\tIf you blast multiple special jewels, you will get additional points for each and every jewel.\r\n✓\tIn order to pass to the next level and win the current round, you need to acquire a certain number of points before the time runs out. The levels get progressively harder as you play on.\r\n✓\tThe final score and the score at the end of each level is calculated by giving a 10000 points bonus for each completed level plus the score obtained at the current level.\r\n\r\n★ Support and Feedback\r\nIf you have any technical problems please email us directly at support@gsoftteam.com.
